ſuccour life beleue reſurreccion deade call vpon thee theſe infantes cummyng thy holy baptiſme may receyue remiſſion ſinnes ſpirituall regeneracion receyue lorde thou haſte promiſed thy welbeloued ſonne ſaying aſke ſhall haue ſeke ſhall finde knocke ſhalbe opened vnto geue nowe vnto v aſke lette v ſeke finde open thy gate vnto v knocke theſe infantes maye enioy euerlaſting benediccion thy heauenly waſhing may come eternall kyngdome whiche thou haſte promyſed chriſte lorde amen let prieſte lokyng vpon child ſaye commaunde thee vnclene ſpirite name father ſonne holy goſte thou come oute departe theſe infantes lorde ieſus chriſte hathe voucheſaued call holye baptiſme made membres bodye holye congregacion therefore thou curſed ſpirit remembre thy ſentence remembre thy iudgement remembre daye hand wherin thou ſhalt burne fyre euerlaſting prepared thee thy aungels preſume hereafter exerciſe anye tirannye towarde theſe infantes chriſte hathe bought precious bloud holy baptiſme calleth flocke ſhall prieſt ſaye lorde people thy ſpirite miniſter ¶heare nowe goſpell written marke marke x certayne tyme broughte child chriſte ſhoulde touche hys dyſciples rebuked thoſe broughte ieſus ſawe diſpleaſed ſayed vnto ſuffre litle child come vnto forbyd ſuche belongeth kyngdome god verely ſay vnto whoſoeuer doeth receyue kyngdome god litle child ſhall entre therin taken vp armes put handes vpō bleſſed goſpell reade miniſter ſhall make thys briefe exhortacion vpon wordes goſpell frendes heare thys goſpell wordes oure sauiour chriſte commaunded child brought vnto hym howe blamed thoſe woulde haue kept hym howe exhorteth menne folowe innocencie ye perceyue howe hys outwarde geſture dede declared hys good wyll towarde embraced armes laied handes vpon thē bleſſed thē doubte ye therfore earneſtlye beleue lykewyſe fauourably receiue theſe preſente infantes embrace armes hys mercy geue vnto bleſſing eternall lyfe make partaker euerlaſting kyngdome wherfore beeing thus perſwaded good heauenlye father toward theſe infantes declared ſonne ieſus chriſt nothyng doubting fauourablye alloweth thys charitable woorke bringyng theſe child holy baptiſme let v faythfully deuoutely geue thankes vnto ſaye prayer whiche lorde himſelfe taught declaracion fayth let v alſo recyte article conteyned crede miniſter godfather godmother people preſent ſhall ſaye ¶our father whiche arte heauen halowed bee thy name c ſhall ſay openly beleue god father almightie c prieſt ſhall adde alſo prayer almyghtie euerlaſting god heauenly father wee geue thee humble thankes thou haſte vouchſaued call v knowledge thy grace faith thee increace cōfirme faith v euermore geue thy holy ſpirit theſe infantes maye bee borne agayne made heyres euerlaſting ſaluacion lorde ieſus chriſte liueth reigneth thee holy ſpirite nowe euer amen let prieſt take one child right hande thother brought cūming churche towarde fonte ſaye lorde vouchſafe receyue hys holy houſholde kepe gouerne alway ſame may haue euerlaſting lyfe amen ſtanding fonte prieſt ſhall ſpeake godfather godmother wiſe welbeloued frendes ye haue brought theſe child bee baptiſed ye haue prayed oure lorde ieſus chriſte woulde vouchſafe receiue laye hys handes vpon bleſſe releaſe theyr ſynnes geue kyngdome heauen euerlaſtyng lyfe ye haue hearde alſo lorde ieſus chriſt hath promiſed goſpel graunt theſe thinges ye haue prayed promiſe parte wil moſte ſurely kepe perfourme wherefore promiſe made chriſte theſe infantes muſt alſo faithfully theyr parte promiſe ſuerties wil forſake deuill hys woorkes conſtantlye beleue woordes n baptize thee c godfather godmother ſhall take laye theyr handes vpon chylde miniſter ſhall put vpon hym hys whyte veſture commonly called criſome ſay take thys whyte veſture token innocencye whiche god grace holy ſacramente baptiſme geuen vnto thee ſygne wherby thou art admoniſhed ſo long thou liueſt geue thy ſelfe innocencie liuing thys tranſitory lyfe thou mayeſt partaker life euerlaſting amen prieſt ſhall annoynte infante vpon head ſaying almightie god father lorde ieſus chriſt hath regenerate thee water holye goſte hath geuen vnto thee remiſſion thy ſinnes voucheſaue annoynte thee vnccyon hys holy ſpirite bring thee inheritance euerlaſting lyfe amen many baptiſed ordre demaunding baptiſyng puttyng criſome enoyntyng ſhalbe vſed ſeuerally euery childe thoſe firſt child haue promiſed forſake deuil woorkes beleue god ſerue hym muſte remember youre partes duetie ſee theſe infantes bee taughte ſo ſoone ſhalbe hable learne ſolemne vowe promyſe profeſſyon haue made maye knowe theſe thynges better ye ſhall call vpon heare ſermons chiefely ſhall prouyde maye learne crede lordes prayer ten commaundementes thengliſhe tonge al thinges whiche chriſtian manne oughte liuing ¶the miniſter ſhall commaunde criſomes bee broughte churche delyuered prieſtes accuſtomed manner purificacyon mother euerye chylde chyldren brought buſſhope bee confirmed hym ſo ſoone ſaye reſonable cauſe declared curate hym approued alſo ſhall warne without great cauſe neceſſitie baptiſe child home theyr houſes great nede ſhal compel ſo doe miniſter thys faſhion ¶firſt let thē preſent whether called vpon god grace ſuccour neceſſitie thyng matter dyd baptiſe childe woordes childe baptiſed whether thinke chylde lawfully perfectly baptiſed yf miniſter ſhall proue aunſwers ſuche brought childe al thinges done ought ſhall chriſten chylde agayne ſhall receyue one flocke true chriſtian people ſaying thus certifye caſe ye haue doen wel accordyng vnto due ordre concernyng euil corrupt affeccions daily proceding al vertue godlines liuyng c publyke baptiſme ¶but yf whiche bryng infantes churche doe make vncertayne aunſwere prieſtes queſtions ſaye cannot tell thought dyd ſayed great feare trouble mynde oftentymes chaunſeth let prieſt baptiſe hym forme aboue wrytten concerninge publyke baptime ſauing dyppyng childe fonte ſhal vſe forme wordes thou baptiſed alreadye n baptize thee name father ſonne holye goſt amen water fonte ſhalbe chaunged euery moneth leaſt afore chyld baptiſed water ſo chaū ged prieſt ſhal ſaye fonte theſe prayer folowyng moſt mercyfull god ſauiour ieſu chriſt haſte ordeyned elemente water regeneracion thy faythfull people vpon beinge baptiſed riuer iordan holye goſte came downe lykenes dooue sende downe beſeche thee ſame thy holy ſpirite aſſiſt v preſent thys inuocacion thy holy name sanctifie ✚ foūtain baptiſme thou art ſanctifier al thinges power thy word thoſe ſhall baptiſed therein may ſpiritually regenerated made child euerlaſtyng adopcion amen mercyful god graunt olde adam ſhalbe baptiſed fountayne may ſo buried newe man may rayſed vp agayne amen graunt carnall affeccions maye die thynges belongyng ſpirite maye lyue growe amen graunte whiche fountayne forſake deuill workes maye haue power ſtrength haue victorye triumph againſt worlde fleſhe amen whoſoeuer ſhall confeſſe thee lord recogniſe alſo thy kingdome amen graunt al ſinne vice maie ſo extinct neuer haue power raigne thy ſeruauntes amē graunte whoſoeuer ſhall begynne thy flocke may euermore continue ſame amen graunt whiche thy ſake lyfe denie forſake themſelfes may wynne purchaſe thee lorde whiche art euerlaſting treaſure amen graunte whoſoeuer dedicated thee office miniſterie may alſo endewed heauenlye vertues euerlaſtinglye rewarded thy mercy bleſſed lorde god doeſt lyue gouerne thinges worlde without ende amen lorde aunſwere thy ſpirite almightie euerliuing god whoſe moſte derely beloued ſonne ieſus chriſt forgeuenes ſinnes ſhead moſt precious ſyde water bloud gaue cōmaundemēt diſciples ſhould goe teache nacions baptiſe name father ſonne holy goſte regarde beſeche thee ſupplycacions thy congregacion graunte thy ſeruauntes whiche ſhall bee baptized water prepared miniſtracion thy holy ſacrament may receiue fulneſſe thy grace euer remaine noumbre thy faithful elect chyldren ieſus chriſt lorde ❧confirmacion❧ wherin conteined cathechiſme child thende confirmacion may miniſtred edifying ſuche ſhall receyue accordyng saint paules doctrine teacheth thynges ſhoulde doen church edificacion ſame thought good none hereafter ſhall confirmed ſuche ſaye mother tong tharticles fayth lordes prayer ten commaūdemētes alſo aunſwere ſuche queſtions ſhort cathechiſme buſhop ſuche ſhall appoynte ſhall hys diſcrecion appoſe thys ordre moſte conueniente obſerued diuers conſideracions ¶firſt becauſe child come yeres diſcrecion haue learned godfather godmother promiſed baptiſme maye themſelfes owne mouthe owne conſent openly churche ratifie confeſſe ſame alſo promiſe grace god wyll euermore endeuour themſelues faythfully obſerue kepe ſuche thinges owne mouth confeſſion haue aſſented vnto ¶secondly aſmuche confirmacion miniſtred baptiſed impoſicion handes prayer may receyue ſtrength defence agaynſt temptacions ſinne aſſautes worlde deuill moſte mete miniſtred child come age partly frayltie owne fleſhe partly aſſautes worlde deuill begyn daungier fall ſynne ¶thirdely agreable vſage churche tymes paſt wherby ordeined confirmacion ſhoulde miniſtred perfecte age beynge inſtructed chriſtes religion ſhoulde openly profeſſe owne fayth promyſe obedyent vnto wyl god ¶and manne ſhall thynke anye detrymente ſhall come child differryng theyr confirmacion ſhal knowe trueth certayn goddes worde chyldren beeyng baptyſed yf departe thys lyfe theyr infancye vndoubtedly ſaued ❧a cathechisme❧ ſay inſtruccion bee learned euery childe brought confirmed buſhop queſtion name aunſwere n queſtion gaue name aunſwere godfather godmother baptiſme wherin made member chriſt child god inheritour kingdome heauen queſtion godfather godmother aunſwere promiſe vowe three thinges name firſt ſhoulde forſake deuill workes pompes vanity wicked worlde ſinneful luſtes fleſhe secondly ſhould beleue article chriſtian faith thirdly ſhould kepe god holy commaundementes walke ſame dayes life queſtion doeſt thou thinke thou art bound beleue doe haue promiſed thee aunſwere yes verely god helpe ſo hartilye thanke heauenly father hath called ſtate ſaluacion ieſus chriſt ſaueour pray god geue grace may continue theſame vnto liues ende queſtion rehearſe article thy beliefe aunſwere beleue god father almightie maker heauen earth ieſus chriſt onely ſonne lord whiche conceyued holy goſt borne virgin marie suffered vnder ponce pilate crucified deade buried deſcended hell thirde day roſe againe dead aſcended heauen ſitteth right hande god father almightie thence ſhal come iudge quicke deade beleue holye goſte holy catholyke churche communion ſainctes forgeuenes ſynnes reſurreccion bodye lyfe euerlaſtinge amen queſtion doeſt thou chiefely learne theſe article thy beliefe aunſwere firſte learne beleue god father hathe made worlde secondly god ſonne hathe redemed mankynde thirdly god holy goſte ſanctifieth electe people god queſtion ſayde godfather godmother dyd promyſe ye ſhoulde kepe goddes commaundementes tell howe many aunſwere tenne queſtion whiche aunſwere thou ſhalte haue none god ii thou ſhalte make thy ſelfe grauen image lykeneſſe thing heauen aboue earth beneath water vnder earth thou ſhalt bow downe thē wurſhip iii thou ſhalt take name lorde thy god vayne iiii remember thou kepe holy sabboth day v honor thy father thy mother vi thou ſhalt doe murdre vii thou ſhalt commit adultry viii thou ſhalt ſteale ix thou ſhalt beare falſe witnes againſt thy neighbour x thou ſhalt couet thy neighbour wyſe ſeruaunt mayde oxe aſſe thing queſtion dooeſt thou chiefely learne theſe commaundementes aunſwere learne two thinges duetie towardes god duetie towardes neighbour queſtion thy duetie towardes god aunſwere duetye towardes god beleue feare loue al heart al minde ſoule ſtrength wurſhip geue thankes put whole truſte call vpon honor holy name worde ſerue truely dayes lyfe queſtion thy duetie towardes thy neighboure aunſwere duetie towardes neighbour loue ſelfe doe men would ſhoulde loue honour ſuccour father mother honour obey kyng miniſters ſubmitte ſelfe gouernours teacher ſpirituall paſtours maiſters ordre ſelfe lowly reuerentlye better hurte bodye woorde dede bee true iuſt dealyng beare malyce hatred heart kepe hādes picking ſtealing tongue euill ſpeaking liyng ſlaundring kepe bodye temperaunce ſobrenes chaſtitie couet deſire men goodes learne laboure truely geate owne liuing duetie ſtate lyfe vnto ſhall pleaſe god cal queſtion good ſonne knowe thou art hable theſe thinges thy ſelfe walke commaundementes god ſerue without ſpeciall grace whiche thou muſte learne good worth chaſtement lord lord loueth chaſtiſeth yea saincte paul ſayeth ſcourgeth euery ſonne whiche receyueth yf endure chaſtiſement offereth himſelfe vnto vnto owne child ſonne father chaſtiſeth
